# [RELEASE 2.10] Release only changes

**Repository:** pytorch  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix



## Description

This is the PyTorch 2.10 release branch CI/CD configuration update. It updates approximately 110 GitHub Actions workflow files under `.github/workflows/` to pin versions, update build matrix references, and adjust CI runner configurations for the 2.10 release branch. The changes are primarily mechanical: updating branch references, Docker image tags, and workflow trigger conditions. This also includes ROCm/HIP-related adjustments for AMD GPU support in the release. Release branch CI configuration must be precise: incorrect workflow pins or build matrix entries can cause nightly builds to fail, release binaries to be built against wrong CUDA/ROCm versions, or tests to run on incorrect infrastructure.

## Task

Changes:
- 110 files modified (primarily `.github/workflows/*.yml`)
- 345 additions, 463 deletions

Tasks:
1. Understand the release branch CI configuration pattern by examining existing workflow files
2. Update workflow files with correct branch references and Docker image tags
3. Adjust build matrix entries for CUDA and ROCm versions
4. Verify your changes compile and match the expected fix

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 110 modified files updated correctly.

## Testing

Your implementation will be automatically verified:

```
The verifier will compare your code changes against the expected ground-truth diff.
Score = 0.35 * file_recall + 0.45 * line_recall + 0.20 * line_precision
```

     1→#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2→#
     3→# Step 2 after branch cut is complete.
     4→#
     5→# Creates PR with release only changes.
     6→#
     7→# Prerequisite: Must be  successfully authenticated in aws fbossci account.
     8→#
     9→# Usage (run from root of project):
    10→#  DRY_RUN=disabled ./scripts/release/apply-release-changes.sh
    11→#
    12→# RELEASE_VERSION: Version of this current release
    13→
    14→set -eou pipefail
    15→
    16→GIT_TOP_DIR=$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)
    17→RELEASE_VERSION=${RELEASE_VERSION:-$(cut -d'.' -f1-2 "${GIT_TOP_DIR}/version.txt")}
    18→DRY_RUN=${DRY_RUN:-enabled}
    19→
    20→echo "Applying to workflows"
    21→for i in .github/workflows/*.yml; do
    22→    sed -i -e s#@main#@"release/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# $i;
    23→done
    24→
    25→echo "Applying to templates"
    26→for i in .github/templates/*.yml.j2; do
    27→    sed -i 's#common.checkout(\(.*\))#common.checkout(\1, checkout_pr_head=False)#' $i;
    28→    sed -i -e s#main#"release/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# $i;
    29→done
    30→
    31→echo "Applying to changes to linux binary builds"
    32→for i in  ".github/workflows/_binary-build-linux.yml" ".github/workflows/_binary-test-linux.yml"; do
    33→    sed -i "/github.event_name == 'pull_request'/d" $i;
    34→    sed -i -e s#main#"release/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# $i;
    35→done
    36→
    37→sed -i -e "/generate_ci_workflows.py/i \\\t\t\t\texport RELEASE_VERSION_TAG=${RELEASE_VERSION}" .github/workflows/lint.yml
    38→
    39→# Triton wheel
    40→echo "Triton Changes"
    41→sed -i -e s#-\ main#"-\ release\/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# .github/workflows/build-triton-wheel.yml
    42→
    43→# XLA related changes
    44→echo "XLA Changes"
    45→sed -i -e s#--quiet#-b\ r"${RELEASE_VERSION}"# .ci/pytorch/

#!/usr/bin/env bash
#
# Step 2 after branch cut is complete.
#
# Creates PR with release only changes.
#
# Prerequisite: Must be  successfully authenticated in aws fbossci account.
#
# Usage (run from root of project):
#  DRY_RUN=disabled ./scripts/release/apply-release-changes.sh
#
# RELEASE_VERSION: Version of this current release

set -eou pipefail

GIT_TOP_DIR=$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)
RELEASE_VERSION=${RELEASE_VERSION:-$(cut -d'.' -f1-2 "${GIT_TOP_DIR}/version.txt")}
DRY_RUN=${DRY_RUN:-enabled}

echo "Applying to workflows"
for i in .github/workflows/*.yml; do
    sed -i -e s#@main#@"release/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# $i;
done

echo "Applying to templates"
for i in .github/templates/*.yml.j2; do
    sed -i 's#common.checkout(\(.*\))#common.checkout(\1, checkout_pr_head=False)#' $i;
    sed -i -e s#main#"release/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# $i;
done

echo "Applying to changes to linux binary builds"
for i in  ".github/workflows/_binary-build-linux.yml" ".github/workflows/_binary-test-linux.yml"; do
    sed -i "/github.event_name == 'pull_request'/d" $i;
    sed -i -e s#main#"release/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# $i;
done

sed -i -e "/generate_ci_workflows.py/i \\\t\t\t\texport RELEASE_VERSION_TAG=${RELEASE_VERSION}" .github/workflows/lint.yml

# Triton wheel
echo "Triton Changes"
sed -i -e s#-\ main#"-\ release\/${RELEASE_VERSION}"# .github/workflows/build-triton-wheel.yml

# XLA related changes
echo "XLA Changes"
sed -i -e s#--quiet#-b\ r"${RELEASE_VERSION}"# .ci/pytorch/common_utils.sh
sed -i -e s#.*#r"${RELEASE_VERSION}"# .github/ci_commit_pins/xla.txt

# Regenerate templates
export RELEASE_VERSION_TAG=${RELEASE_VERSION}
./.github/regenerate.sh

# Pin Unstable and disabled jobs and tests
UNSTABLE_VER=$(aws s3api list-object-versions --bucket ossci-metrics --prefix unstable-jobs.

function clone_pytorch_xla() {
  if [[ ! -d ./xla ]]; then
    git clone --recursive -b r2.10 https://github.com/pytorch/xla.git
    pushd xla
    # pin the xla hash so that we don't get broken by changes to xla
    git checkout "$(cat ../.github/ci_commit_pins/xla.txt)"

echo "Generated workflow files for nightly: $(ls /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-*-nightly.yml 2>/dev/null | wc -l)"
echo "Generated workflow files for release: $(ls /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-*-release*.yml 2>/dev/null | wc -l)"

74. $ 
ls /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-*release*.yml

75. $ 
# Check if there's any documentation about the release process
find /workspace -name "RELEASE*" -o -name "*release*" -path "*doc*" | grep -i "guide\|readme\|doc" | head -10

76. $ 
# Get the content of a nightly generated file
cp /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-nightly.yml /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-release-2-10.yml

# Now modify the key parts
sed -i 's/branches:\s*-\s*nightly/branches:\n      - release\/2.10/' /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-release-2-10.yml

# Check the modification
grep -A 5 "on:" /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-release-2-10.yml | head -10

77. $ 
# Delete the manually created file
rm /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-release-2-10.yml

# Check what we deleted
git status | head -5

78. $ 
cat > /tmp/generate_release_workflows.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
# Generate release/2.10 branch workflows by copying nightly versions

cd /workspace/.github/workflows

for nightly_file in generated-*-nightly.yml; do
  # Create release version by replacing 'nightly' with 'release-2-10' in filename
  release_file="${nightly_file%-nightly.yml}-release-2-10.yml"
  
  # Copy the file
  cp "$nightly_file" "$release_file"
  
  # Replace nightly branch with release/2.10 branch
  sed -i 's/- nightly$/- release\/2.10/' "$release_file"
  
  # Remove the nightly-specific comment
  sed -i '/NOTE: Meta Employees can trigger new nightlies/d' "$release_file"
  
  echo "Created $release_file"
done
EOF

chmod +x /tmp/generate_release_workflows.sh
/tmp/generate_release_workflows.sh

79. $ 
# Check git status
git status --short | head -20

80. $ 
# Add all the new files to git
git add .github/workflows/generated-*-release-2-10.yml

# Check the status
git status --short | wc -l

81. $ 
# Check the diff stats
git diff --cached --stat | tail -20

82. $ 
# Check the branches in one of the generated files
grep -A 2 "on:" /workspace/.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-release-2-10.yml | head -10

83. $ 
# Check if generated files are in .gitignore
cat /workspace/.github/.gitignore 2>/dev/null || echo "No .gitignore in .github"

84. $ 
grep -n "generated\|\.github/workflows" /workspace/.gitignore | head -20

85. $ 
# Check total changes
git diff --cached --stat | tail -5

86. $ 
# Remove the generated files from staging and delete them
git reset HEAD .github/workflows/generated-*-release-2-10.yml
rm .github/workflows/generated-*-release-2-10.yml

# Check status
git status

87. $ 
# Check recent git history
git log --oneline -10

88. $ 
# Final verification of release 2.10 configuration
echo "=== Final Release 2.10 Configuration Verification ==="
echo
echo "1. Workflow files with @release/2.10:"
grep -l "@release/2.10" /workspace/.github/workflows/*.yml | wc -l
echo
echo "2. Files with main references that should be release/2.10 (excluding infrastructure):"
for file in /workspace/.github/workflows/*.yml; do
  if ! grep -q "@release" "$file"; then
    basename "$file"
  fi
done | grep -v "check-labels\|docathon\|docker-cache\|docker-release\|llm_td\|nitpicker\|scorecards\|trymerge\|weekly\|nightly" | head -10
echo
echo "3. Key configuration files verification:"
echo "  - lint.yml RELEASE_VERSION_TAG: $(grep -c 'RELEASE_VERSION_TAG=2.10' /workspace/.github/workflows/lint.yml)"
echo "  - XLA r2.10: $(grep -c 'r2.10' /workspace/.github/ci_commit_pins/xla.txt)"
echo "  - Common utils XLA: $(grep -c '\-b r2.10' /workspace/.ci/pytorch/common_utils.sh)"
echo "  - Triton release/2.10: $(grep -c 'release/2.10' /workspace/.github/workflows/build-triton-wheel.yml)"
echo
echo "4. S3 version IDs pinned:"
grep -c "versionId=" /workspace/.github/scripts/filter_test_configs.py
echo
echo "Current git status:"
git status --short | wc -l
